The lyrics also have a good amount of meaning behind them unlike the rest of Imagine Dragons output. 0:09 - 0:32 Can be easily interpreted as him talking about his career, also Wellbutrin is a discontinued drug made to treat depression. 0:21 Can also be interpreted as starting drama for attention like how many famous people thrive off of rumors. 1:01 Gethsemane means "Oil press" but is more probably talking about the Garden of Gethsemane, where Jesus was arrested, but also frequented, this lyric can be interpreted in a few ways, but I personally believe that the interpreted as: He is building the place where he is going to fall from a young age. After this the lyrics are pretty simple but stable metaphors.  PS: I really like small voice tick at 0:29 to symbolize a clock ticking.

Thank you all for coming. Weâ€™re gathered here today to honor the memory of a once great rock and roll band. One that was supposed to bring true rock n roll back into the spot light. In a world drowning in pop and hip hop on the billboard hot 100, this band was supposed to be the only shining example that rock and roll was still alive and could still be relevant. For years they waged this just and righteous war, introducing rock music to the next generation.   Alas, the fight proved to be just too much. Songs once teaming with life, emotion, and passion turned into a barren wasteland of garage band drums, piano, and synth. Songs that once featured the thoughts and ideas of all 4 members of the band now seem to be hijacked by the maniacal pop ambitions of a madman.   We take this time to remember imagine dragons not as they are, but as they once were. Itâ€™s been a great ride but Where as today it is Imagine Dragons, we all shall fall. May God have mercy on them so one day they may crawl back from the abyss. But you either die a hero or live long enough to see yourself become the villain. Thank you, and good night.
